- **7518**: Proceeding with the Aht Urhgan mission "Path of Darkness" will prevent you from entering Salaheem's Sentinels until the mission is complete.
- **7519**: You can now proceed with the Aht Urhgan mission "Nashmeira's Plea."
- **7520**: Do you wish to proceed with the mission?
- **7521**: Proceed with the mission? [Yes./No.]
- **7683**: @ @@ Once there was a meeting of two great masses. @
- **7684**: @ @@ One, an entity of "dark." @
- **7685**: @ @@ One, an entity of "light." @
- **7686**: @ @@ Their collision gave birth to a violent storm.
- **7687**: @ @@ The storm rose towards the heavens, and burst into a million fragments. @
- **7688**: @@
